 Qureshi took over as the 17th Chief Election Commissioner of the country on Friday
 unhone is pad par naveen chawla kaa sthaan liya he, jo guuruuvaar ko sevanivruth ho gayi
 The notification of the appointment of Senior Election Commissioner Qureshi as Chief Election Commissioner in the three-member Election Commission was issued on July 27

 billi kii tarah hi sher, chita, tendua samet kai anya jaanwaron kii aakhen raat main chamakati hai
 Do you know why this happens? Animals whose eyes are shining have a thin layer of a special type of crystalline sbstance in their eyes
 yah patali parat ankhon par padane vaale prakaash ko paravartit kar detii he
 This is the same type of action as when a ray of sun starts shining on a mirror
 vahiin, billi kiankhon par kiye gaye ek prayogse pataa chalata he ki uski ankhon ke parde ke peeche ekachmakdaar padaarthki parat hoti he, jise luminius teppetom (luminous tepetum) kehete hai
 This substance reflects light
 is parat ke kaaran bahut kam roshni main bhi billi aasaani se chizon ko dekh leti he
 All those animals whose eyes glow in the night can see well in the darkness
 iske alaava ek or baat gaur karne laayak he ki jinjanwaron kii ankhenraat main chamakati he, un sabaki chamak kaa rang ek jaisaa nahin hota he

 Jagmohan Dalmiya, not only the BCCI, has also been the President of the International Cricket Council (ICC) and he is credited with earning cricket in India, but he had to lose the position seven years ago due to allegations of financial irregularities
 kolkata ke rahane vaale daalamia varsh 1979 main bisisiai se jude the or apane dost se baad main dushman bane inderjeet singh bindra ke saath apni chhap chodi
 Both played a key role in organizing the one-day Cricket World Cup in India and commercialized the game

 unhen haalanki tivi adhikaron kii bikri ko lekar hue vivaad ke kaaran isisi kaa pad chhodana padaa tha

 unka vah kaarykaal varsh 2004 main khatm hua, lekin unke samarthit ummidavaar haryana ke ranbir singh mahendra ne maharashtra ke kaddavar netaa sharad pavaar ko haraakar adhyaksh pad hasil kar liya

 Dalmiya, who hails from Kolkata, joined the BCCI in the year 1979 and left his mark with his friend, later turned enemy Inderjit Singh Bindra
 donon ne bharat main ek-divasiy cricket vishwacap ke aayojan main ahm bhoomika nibhaai or khel kaa vyavsaayeekaran kiya
